<script src="http://assets.dwstatic.com/common/js/jquery.js"></script>
<script>
$(function(){
    //加载相关视频
        var jsapi = 'http://video.duowan.com/jsapi/';
        var hotUser = {

            checkUrl : function (href){
                var regExp = /video\.duowan\.com\/(\w+)\/.*/g;
                return regExp.exec(href);
            },

            getChannel : function (href){
                //获取频道
                if ( href == '' || typeof(href) == "undefined") {
                    href = window.location.href;
                }
                var channelArr = ['ycvideo', 'lol' , 'dnf' , 'yule', 'wot' , 'mc' ,'cf' , 'dota2', 'pc' , 'wow', 'coc', 'ls', 'd3', 'fbyx' , 'wuxia' , 'age' , 'nz' ,'cod' , 'wows' , 'smite' , 'bb' , 'hyty' , 'anime', 'csgo',];
                result = this.checkUrl(href);
                //判断是否有符合要求数据
                if( result[1] == ''){
                   return 'duowanvideo';
                }else{
                    //是否在数组中
                  if( $.inArray(result[1], channelArr) != '-1' ){
                      return result[1];
                  }else{
                    //如果不是频道页则其他处理
                    if( 'play' == result[1] ){
                        //播放页处理取面包屑内容
                        var url = $('.crumbs a').eq(0).attr('href');
                        if (url != '' && typeof(url) != "undefined" ) {
                            return this.getChannel(url);
                        }else{
                            return 'duowanvideo';
                        }
                    }else{
                        //其他页面默认为多玩视频专区
                        return 'duowanvideo';
                    }
                  }
                } 
            },
        

            renderData : function(channel){
                //接口获取数据
                 $.post(jsapi+'getusersbyfilter', {channel:channel}, function(data){
                    //console.log(data);
                    var html = '';
                   if (data) {
                        for(var i=0; i<data.length; i++){ 
                            html +=  '<li><a href="'+data[i]['user_homepage']+'"><img src="'+data[i]['user_avatar']+'" alt="'+data[i]['user_nickname']+'" class="fltL"/> <p>'+data[i]['user_nickname']+'</p> <blockquote>'+data[i]['user_channel_name']+'</blockquote></a></li>';
                        }
                        $("#userRecommend").html(html);
                    }
              },'json');
            },

            init: function(){
                try{
                    var channel = this.getChannel();
                    this.renderData(channel); 
                }catch(e){}          
            }
        };   
        hotUser.init();
})    
</script>

<script>
    seajs.use(['$', 'gallery/underscore/1.6.0/underscore'], function ($, _) {
        $(window).resize(debounce(function (event) {
            if ($(window).width() < 1340) {
                $('body').addClass('layout-small')
            } else {
                $('body').removeClass('layout-small')
            }
        }, 300))

        function debounce(func, wait, immediate) {
            var timeout;
            return function () {
                var context = this,
                        args = arguments;
                var later = function () {
                    timeout = null;
                    if (!immediate) func.apply(context, args);
                };
                var callNow = immediate && !timeout;
                clearTimeout(timeout);
                timeout = setTimeout(later, wait);
                if (callNow) func.apply(context, args);
            };
        }

    })
    seajs.use(['p/huyavod/sidebar/1.0.3/sidebar'], function (Sidebar) {
        //var sb = new Sidebar() ; 暂时禁用侧边栏
